#### Opcodes

```
  0: 0x21EA [0x20] SET_CLI_EVENT_UC_FLAG: Lock player control
  1: 0x21EC [0x48] [System] [7624*]:
    → "This device appears to be connected to the level above."
  2: 0x21EF [0x23] WAIT_FOR_DIALOG_INTERACTION
  3: 0x21F0 [0x24] CREATE_DIALOG(message_id=7625*, default_option=1*, option_flags=0*)
    → "Use the device? [Yes./No.]"
  4: 0x21F7 [0x25] WAIT_DIALOG_SELECT()
  5: 0x21F8 [0x02] IF !(Work_Zone[0] == 0*) GOTO 0x2214
  6: 0x2200 [0x42] SET_CLI_EVENT_CANCEL_DATA()
  7: 0x2201 [0x43] SEND_EVENT_UPDATE: Send pending tag to server (packet 0x005B)
  8: 0x2203 [0x43] SEND_EVENT_UPDATE: Check pending flag (skip if not pending)
  9: 0x2205 [0x03] Work_Zone[1] = 1*
 10: 0x220A [0x29] REQ_SET_WAIT(priority=0x01, entity_id=LocalPlayer, tag_num=0x08)
 11: 0x2211 [0x01] GOTO 0x221F
 12: 0x2214 [0x02] IF !(Work_Zone[0] == 1*) GOTO 0x221F
 13: 0x221C [0x01] GOTO 0x221F

SUBROUTINE_221F:
 14: 0x221F [0x20] SET_CLI_EVENT_UC_FLAG: Unlock player control
 15: 0x2221 [0x21] END_EVENT
 16: 0x2222 [0x00] END_REQSTACK()
```
